SELECT [p].[Id] AS [ProductId], [s].[Name] AS [ShopName], [c].[Name] AS [CategoryName], [p].[Name] AS [ProductName], [p].[ImageUrl], [p].[Price], [p].[Color], [p].[Stock]
FROM [Products] AS [p]
